[23/08/23, 4:44:08 PM] ~ Deep: As our 𝐍𝐒𝐒 𝐯𝐨𝐥𝐮𝐧𝐭𝐞𝐞𝐫 𝐫𝐞𝐠𝐢𝐬𝐭𝐫𝐚𝐭𝐢𝐨𝐧 𝐝𝐫𝐢𝐯𝐞 kicks off tomorrow, we want to address a few concerns or uncertainties that you may have by providing a list of frequently asked questions ‼️

*What do we expect from DJSNSS volunteers?* 👀 
➡️Volunteers are expected to attend all DJSNSS events, including the annual camp, to complete 120 𝒉𝒐𝒖𝒓𝒔 of service per year. Punctuality and discipline are highly valued ⭐

*How long are volunteers committed to DJSNSS?* 🤔💭
➡️Volunteering for NSS requires a 𝑡𝑤𝑜-𝑦𝑒𝑎𝑟 𝑐𝑜𝑚𝑚𝑖𝑡𝑚𝑒𝑛𝑡, with 120 hours of service per year, for a total of 240 hours 😁🤝🏻

*How often are events scheduled?* 🧐⏱️
➡️Typically, we conduct 2-3 events per month, mostly 𝘰𝘯 𝘚𝘶𝘯𝘥𝘢𝘺𝘴. However, no events will be scheduled during Term Tests and End Semesters 📆

*Will I receive any certificate or grace marks for my service at NSS?* 🫣📄
➡️Yes, you will be eligible to get 10 marks only if you complete 120 hours of service. These 10 marks will be added to your even semesters. If you want to obtain the University NSS Certificate, you'll need to complete 240 𝒉𝒐𝒖𝒓𝒔 𝒐𝒇 𝒔𝒆𝒓𝒗𝒊𝒄𝒆 and attend one annual camp during two years of volunteering 🥳🚀

*What are the requirements for registration?* 🧾🎯
You need to bring
➡️ 𝟮 𝗽𝗵𝗼𝘁𝗼𝘀 smaller in size than passport size.
➡️ 𝟐 𝐜𝐨𝐩𝐢𝐞𝐬 𝐨𝐟 𝐭𝐡𝐞 𝐫𝐞𝐠𝐢𝐬𝐭𝐫𝐚𝐭𝐢𝐨𝐧 𝐟𝐨𝐫𝐦 which is available at the 4th-floor Xerox shop.

Guess what? It’s that time of the year we’ve all been waiting for 🤩
Unleash your winter wanderlust and join us on the most thrilling adventure of January 2024 - the "Winter Trip to Himachal Pradesh" with BackPacker Tours 🎒

Here's a sneak peek at what you absolutely don't want to miss:

🌅 Golden Temple at Night: Imagine standing before the enchanting Golden Temple in Amritsar under the shimmering moonlight, a truly magical experience.

🎆 Wagah Border Ceremony: Feel the patriotic fervor as you witness the Indian and Pakistani armies' Flag Down Ceremony. The energy here is electrifying!

🏞️ Manali Adventures: Paragliding in Solang Valley, DJ nights under the starry Himalayan sky, and relaxing at the hot water springs of Vashisht Temple.

🛣️ Atal Tunnel: Explore this engineering marvel, and take a detour to the picturesque village of Sissu.

🌄 Camping in Kasol: Connect with nature as you camp by the Parvati River in the tranquil Parvati Valley. Explore, hike, and soak in the serene surroundings.

🕍 Manikaran Gurudwara: Witness a unique spiritual experience as a langar is prepared in a hot water spring, nestled in the lap of nature.

🌊 River Rafting and Paragliding in Kullu: Get your adrenaline pumping with these thrilling activities in the beautiful Kullu Valley.

🏞️ Tranquility at Sukhna Lake: In Chandigarh, take in the picturesque Sukhna Lake's serenity before heading back.

Don't miss out on the adventure of a lifetime! Join us for an epic journey through Himachal Pradesh. Excitement is building up, and the fear of missing out is real ‼️
Contact us to secure your spot at the earliest and be a part of this epic journey! 🎉🌄 #HimachalWinterTrip

We're happy to open applications for the *Finlatics Financial Markets Experience Program*, an online *live project* that helps students *gain work experience* in *financial markets* at the *Dwarkadas Jivanlal Sanghvi College of Engineering*.

*No prior domain knowledge* is required to be a part of the project as it includes personalized *mentoring*, guidance and *live sessions* to train students.

Benefits post completion: 
1. *Certificate of Work  Experience*
2. *Letter of Recommendation*.

The project runs at leading institutes including *IIT Delhi*, *IIT Bombay*, *IIT Madras*, *VJTI Mumbai* and *BITS Pilani* among others.

To apply, please use the link below:

https://www.finlatics.com/smscampain/application/index.php?utm_src=djsce

*Project Duration* : 2 months

*Project start*: Flexible on student choice. To *balance* it along with exams or assignments, students can choose to start it once they are completed. 

*Project Break*: Students can also take a break on the project in case they need it for exams or assignment. 

If selected, the program has a minimal induction fee:  Rs. 1999 + GST / Rs. 2999 + GST (on student choice)

*Fee Waiver*: A fee waiver in the range of *25-30%* shall be given to all *Dwarkadas Jivanlal Sanghvi College of Engineering* students on the abovementioned minimal induction fee. This will *reduce the fee* to Rs. 1499 + GST / Rs. 2049 + GST.

To be eligible for the fee waiver, kindly apply through the abovementioned link only.

*No payment* has to be made right now

*Incentives* : upto Rs. 6000 (for top performers) 

The *application* process would take *2-3 mins* of your time.

We are pleased to open applications at *Dwarkadas J. Sanghvi College of Engineering, Mumbai* for the *Finlatics Business Analyst Experience Program*, an *online Live Project* that helps you gain work experience in *data-driven decision making*. 

The program uses a *case study-driven approach*, where you will *assess business projects* and *solve problems* using models used by leading consulting firms like *Zomato & Accenture*. You'll also learn *Power BI*, a business intelligence tool, and use it on actual *sales data* to gain insights.

To apply, students can fill out the form below and we'll get in touch with them:

https://www.finlatics.com/ba/application/index.php?utm_src=djsce

*Benefits* post completion: 
* *Certificate of Work Experience*
* *Letter of Recommendation*

*Program Duration* : 1 month / 2 months (on student choice)

*Program Start*: Flexible on student choice. Can be started *post exams*. 

This project is running at *leading campuses* including *IIT Bombay, IIT Delhi, IIT Madras, VJTI Mumbai and BITS Pilani* among others.

*No pre-requisites* or prior domain knowledge is required to be a part of the program and all necessary training on data-driven decision-making & Power BI will be imparted on the program.

The program will also have *live sessions* to cover additional business cases. 

*Time Commitment*: 2 - 4 hours per week

If selected, the program has a minimal induction fee of Rs. 2999 + GST / 1999 + GST (on student choice)

*Fee Waiver*:  A *fee waiver of 25 - 30%* shall be given to all *Dwarkadas J. Sanghvi College of Engineering, Mumbai*  students on the abovementioned minimal induction fee. This waiver will *reduce the fee* to Rs. 1499 + GST / Rs. 2049 + GST. 

To be eligible for the fee waiver, kindly apply through the abovementioned link only.

[16/04/24, 11:41:56 PM] ~ VK ARMY ✌🏻💜: The Internship Fair (IF) is a premier event, emphasizing the practical application of academic knowledge for professional growth. We urge all DJSCE students (FEs, SEs, and TEs) to participate and discover their interests through internship opportunities. Remember, IF applications are exclusively for DJSCE students in their first, second, and third years. Embrace this chance to embark on your professional journey.

Please go through the following RULES & REGULATIONS:

●The duration of the internship may range from one to three months (online/offline/Hybrid
mode), commencing after your semester exams, and can be extended to PPO depending upon
the convenience of the company and the candidates.
● The internship may be part time or online mode for the duration of semester, else full-
time(online/offline) during the course of vacation, depending on the recruiting company’s requirements.
● Registrations are open till 30th April, 11:59pm.
● The registration form can only be filled once.
● Although you will be allowed to apply for multiple companies , once shortlisting is done , you
will be allowed to sit only for 2 interviews . So, be sure to check the Job descriptions/
conditions in detail before applying.
● It is important to note that the first offer that the candidate receives, he/she must accept that
offer, regardless of the stipend amount .
● After the selection process, if any company request payment, please notify the IF organizing
committee without delay.
● The company registration form asks for a drive link to your resume, so please make sure that you have your resume
ready and uploaded on the drive while you are applying. Do ensure that the link is not private.
The resume should be uploaded in pdf format with name format Name_Year_Dept_SAPId
● The interviews will be held on 3rd and 4th May , 2024 from 9am - 7pm. They will be either
conducted online (gmeet) or offline (In College) depending upon the company's preference.
The schedule for the interviews along with the mode will be released on our website, whatsapp
group & our app as soon as the details are received by our team from the company.
● Please ensure that you are on time for all your interview slots, DJSCE IF organizing committee
will not be responsible for missed interviews.

SE whatsapp group link - 
https://chat.whatsapp.com/LJTLjzYzj6cJ7TDINtSTI7
